# OpenLibrary "poisoned guard" contamination audit

Generated by scripts/_audit_ol_contamination.ts (read-only). Re-applies the
corrected un-poisoned guard to every stored openlibrary description.

Total openlibrary descriptions scanned: **3542**

| binding | total | rejected by fixed guard |
|---|---:|---:|
| isbn | 3354 | 2814 |
| work_id | 118 | 63 |
| search | 70 | 64 |

**Total contaminated: 2941**

These descriptions do not mention their book's own title or author and
would be rejected by the fixed pipeline. Recommended remediation: clear
description_book + provenance and set data_quality_status='flagged' so the
fixed pipeline re-enriches them from a verified source.
